[MBO-04(1)-1]
<H>{@sāraḷā mahābhārata
<>banaparba
<>pāṇḍabaṅka banabāsa@}
<P>jaẏatu bāsudeba kamaḷā biḷāsa
<P>to nāma sumarante baikuṇṭhe bāsa | 1 |
<P>sehi pādapadme nityeheṁ śaraṇa
<P>śūdramuni sāroḷa dāsa sebe se debī caraṇa | 2 |
<P>baibasuta manu agastiṁki kale pucchā
<P>pāṇḍabe kaurobe kemante hoile ye kakṣā | 3 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi banabase rahile kemante
<P>ẏethira prastāba muni kahibāka mote | 4 |
<P>śuṇa āho baibasuta bidanti agasti
<P>pāṇḍabongka banabāsa helā yeuṁ mati | 5 |
<P>aneka sānande ye dharmara nandana
<P>śutra rohiṇī yoge kaleka parasthāna | 6 |
<P>tuḷamāsa kr̥ṣṇapakṣa puṇa budhabāra
<P>amr̥ta yoga rohiṇī br̥ṣa aṭai se dinara | 7 |
<P>bāḷaba nāme karaṇa byatipāta nāme yoga
<P>pañchamī tithi sedina pāṇḍabe paśile banamārga | 8 |
[MBO-04(1)-2]
<P>prathama dine rahile indra ye praśaste
<P>dhaśāsana goḍāi acchi karṇṇa śakuni sahite | 9 |
<P>dhana ratnamāna na puṇa nianti se bane
<P>samasta chaḍāi gheni boli āgyāṁ dilā driyodhana | 10 |
<P>indrapraśastuṁ bāhāra hoile bahana
<P>āu dine bāruṇābante karanti gamana | 11 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi bhīma arjuna nakuḷa sahadeba
<P>kointā dropatī, subhadrākaiṁ gheniṇa caḷanti pañchu ye pāṇḍaba | 12 |
<P>suranadīra tīre caḷanti pañchu bīre
<P>tr̥tīẏa dine prabeśa manohara banastare | 13 |
<P>aṁgeṇa thilā tāṁkara yeteka aḷaṁkāramāna
<P>samasta śodhiṇa ye ghenilā dhuśāsana | 14 |
<P>bhīmasenara śarīra kampai ati rāge
<P>dhuśāsanakaiṁ prahāra ki kariba sāṣṭāṁge | 15 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile kopa na kara re bhīma
<P>ucita kathāku bābu kimpe karu tama | 16 |
<P>bābu driyodhana boli kari yeuṁṇa mora bhrāta
<P>temanta sodara āmbhanta janme janme hou prāpata | 17 |
<P>aḷaṁkāramāna yebe āmbhara tahiṁ thānā
<P>banastare abaśya ye pramāda āmbhnta paḍanā | 18 |
<P>bābu bipada kāḷakaiṁ dhana sundara bhāriyā
<P>paṇḍita jane ẏehākaiṁ karanti paritejyā | 19 |
<P>āmbhara se dhana basra saḷaṁkāra bkeheneke nebā
<P>bābu banabāsuṁ aile puṇa loḍile pāibā | 20 |
<P>bābu āpaṇā karma bipākare kimpe pare dvandī
<P>āpaṇe apaṇḍitare pare kimpā nindi | 21 |
<P>āpaṇe prahāraji kariba animite | 22 |
[MBO-04(1)-3]
<P>ẏehā tu bicāra re na karu kimpe mane
<P>anubrate mūrkhapaṇe bratibu kesane | 23 |
<P>bābu ẏebe subuddhipaṇa karithāa bratibāku
<P>yemante ripu kaḷi nuāranti āmbhaṁku | 24 |
<P>dhuśāsana karṇṇa śakuniki bāhuḍāi
<P>takṣaka bane bijaẏa kale bege yāṁ | 25 |
<P>asakate chāli nuāranti debī kointe
<P>nirjhara jhara se ye gahana banaste | 26 |
<P>se dina rahile yāiṁ bārāhī nadī kūḷe
<P>rātreka bañchile se nimba br̥kṣa teḷe | 27 |
<P>biharanti rātrakāḷe ramabeṇṭa pāridhi
<P>hariṇī bāhuṭiā nānā jībanta binddha | 28 |
<P>ẏemante pāṇḍabe ye bihaḍanti bane
<P>tahuṁ yāiṁ biśrāmile kāmyaka nāme araṇye | 29 |
<P>karṇṇakeśarī boli ẏeka nadī goṭi |
<P>mekhaḷī gaṅgāru se tini dhāra phuṭi | 30
<P>kāmyaka boli kari ẏekai pabongta
<P>thaḷa uccharga se aṭai juṇa sāta | 31 |
<P>yamadagni nidhane praśurāma tapobante
<P>kāmya śrāddha kale tahīm deba pitr̥kāryya arthe | 32 |
<P>teṇu se kāmyeka boli nāma parasiddhi
<P>se parabate thile pañchumana hoẏe sādhi | 33 |
<P>se bana parimaḷa dekhi rahile yujheṣṭhi
<P>se kāmyeka pabongta upare rañchile parṇṇakuṭī | 34 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile śuṇa re pārthiba |
<P>arṇyaku yibā yebe kahibā bāsudeba | 35 |
<P>hariṁki sumaraṇā tu ho karasi bīra pārtha
<P>tāhāṁkara āge kahibā nā samasta br̥ttānta | 36 |
[MBO-04(1)-4]
<P>svāmīkara āgyāṁ ye pāiṇa dhanurjaẏe
<P>saurabha pātre jaḷa bhari kr̥ṣṇaṁku kalā dhyāẏe | 37 |
<P>mana bacana karttabye kr̥ṣṇaṁku dhyāẏe karai
<P>nārāẏaṇa padapadme laẏe bāsaba tanaẏi | 38 |
<P>candraśāḷā mandire se bijaẏe janārddana
<P>arjunara cintante debaṁkara ṭaḷilā āsana | 39 |
<P>dhyāneṇa jāṇile se deba ye gobinda
<P>bichāranti pāṇḍabanta paḍilā paramāda | 40 |
<P>bainetraku sumaraṇā kale catradhārī
<P>ramyaka dīparu āsi baineta bije kari | 41 |
<P>bijaẏa nārāẏaṇa bainetra piṭhi
<P>prabeśa kāmyeka bane pahiṁ bijaẏa karichanti yujheṣṭhi | 42 |
<P>bainetra pithiru uturile deba catrapāṇi
<P>yujheṣthiṁka chāmure deba bije brahmāṇḍa śiromaṇi | 43 |
<P>yujheṣṭhiṁka mukha chāhiṁṇa deba ye acyute
<P>śate sahasra daṇḍa pralamba karanti jagannāthe | 44 |
<P>uṭhiṇa yujheṣṭhi jagannāṭhakaiṁ kale koḷa
<P>dekhiṇa biṣāda hele debīṁkara bāḷa | 45 |
<P>svāmī ẏe durāpada ghora dusaha banaste
<P>ẏe nirjhara jhara banaste paśila kimarthe | 46 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi deba boile śuṇimā debarāja
<P>paśāra kutuhoḷe ye harāili sama rājya | 47 |
<P>yujheṣṭhiṁka bacana śuṇi deba sumarile byāsa mahāruṣi
<P>kāmyaka bane byāse prabeśa hoile āsi | 48 |
<P1>37–svāmīṁkara āgyāṁ ye pāiṇa bīra pātha
<>śaucabanta hoi harili sumara turita |–ja
<P1>37|2–śāucabanta hoi kr̥ṣṇaṁku laẏa kara ẏekānta |–ja, jha
[MBO-04(1)-5]
<P>tuleṇa achanti tāṁka ṣāṭhiẏe sahasa śiṣi
<P>bāḷakhilyāmānanta gheni prabeśa hele āsi | 49 |
<P>dharmaṁkara nandana ye uṭhile dhātikāre
<P>karanti pūjā bidhi byāsaṁka paẏare | 50 |
<P>gobinde boile śuṇimā muni byās
<P>yujheṣṭhi debongkara hāde puṇihiṁ banabāsa | 51 |
<P>byāse boile hari tote keuṇa kathā dullabha
<P>yeuṇa arthe yujheṣṭhi banabāsa na jāṇu ki bāsudeba | 52 |
<P>kīcaka bhārā ye na sahilā basumatī
<P>agyāṁtabāse birāṭa rājyare bañchibe yujheṣṭhi nr̥pati | 53 |
<P>dropatīra arthe ye bahda kīcaka nr̥apatya
<P>ballabha rūpe bhīma māriba kīcaka śatebhrāta | 54 |
<P>tada nimante yujheṣthi hoile banabāsī
<P>śuṇi kari haraṣa hile ye hr̥ṣikeśi | 55 |
<P>kāmyaka bane rahile hari beni māsa
<P>ẏemanteṇa galā ye keteka dibasa | 56 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi bolanti śuṇa he acyuta
<P>tumbhara tule nia āmbha kointā ye māta | 57 |
<P1>56|1–“māmyaka bane rahile hari beni māsa” pāṭha pare ‘ṭha’
<>pothire adhikā pāṭha :–
<P1>kāmyaka bane rahile hari beni māsa
<P1>tahuṁ dvārikāku bije kale hr̥ṣīkeśa |
<P1>kuntīdebī boile ye śrīhariṁki chāhiṁ
<P1>subhadrāra garbha pāñchamāsa acchi hoi |
<P1>kemante rahiba bane nuhai yukata
<P1>saṅgatare dvārikāku nia śirīpati |
<P1>muhiṁ br̥ddhakāḷe bane nuāribi chāli
<P1>bidura ghare rahibi śokaku sambhāḷi |
<P1>subhadrāku saṅge gheni bije kale hari
<P1>antara hoile tahuṁ byāsa tapachārī |
[MBO-04(1)-6]
<P>tumbhar abhaginī ye ābara bropatī
<P>tāhānta nia boli boile yujheṣṭhi nr̥pati | 58 |
<P>gobinde boile dropatī nimante banabāsa
<P>tāhāra hetu se kīcaka yiba nāśa | 59 |
<P>subhadrā kointāku gheni āmbhe yibu
<P>bidura ghare nei kointāṁku chāḍibu | 60 |
<P>ẏete bichāri deba beniṁki gheni aile
<P>dropatīki gheni pāṇḍabe banaste rahile | 61 |
<P>pāñchāḷī kumāraṁku chāḍile dr̥padara ghare
<P>ẏesaneka pāṇḍabe paśile banastare | 62 |
<P>āho pāṇḍabaṁkara tule ye bidare thile rahi
<P>sarasvatīru tāṁku paṭhāile bāhuḍāi | 63 |
<P>bāhuḍanti bidure ye paṇḍita mahāyodhī
<P>sodara biartheṇa śarīra baḍa trodhī | 64 |
<P>āsane bijekari achanti dhr̥tarāṣṭa
<P>ẏemaneka samaẏe bidure hoile yāiṁ bheṭa | 65 |
<P>dhr̥tarāṣṭa caraṇe bidura pariṇāmi
<P>sañjaẏe boile abadhāna karibā debasvāmī | 66 |
<P>bidure daraśana karuacchi kurupati
<P>dhr̥tarāṣṭe boile bidura mora kati | 67 |
<P>tu ye goḍāilu poaṁkara tuḷe
<P>kesane rūpa hoi banabāsa gale | 68 |
<P>bidure kahile dhr̥tarāṣṭaṁkara pāśa
<P>dekhantā lokaṁkara mana baḍāi birasa | 69 |
<P>tāhāṁkara mane deba antara kicchi nāhiṁ
<P>mahā phuruṇā hoi caḷanti gaṇagāhī | 70 |
<P>puṇa puṇa biduraku pachārai dhr̥tirāṣṭi
<P>kesaneka rūpe ẏethuṁ galāka yujhesthi | 71 |
[MBO-04(1)-7]
<P>ambubatīta nandnna kahai karayoḍi
<P>odā basra ẏeka inddha odā basra ẏeka oḍi | 72 |
<P>heṭhamātha hoi caḷai dharmasuta
<P>bhūmiki niropi se yesane maẏematta | 73 |
<P>svāmī kuṭumba loke mr̥tu hoibāra parāẏe
<P>sehi sarūpeṇa cālai kontīra tanaẏe | 74 |
<P>śuṇiṇa dhr̥tarāṣṭa birasa kale mana
<P>kehneka sarūpe bāhāra hela bhīmasena | 75 |
<P>bidura kahile sabu bhīmasenara kathā
<P>tāhāra biśvamūrtti chāḍai ki sarbathā | 76 |
<P>bhmaja bistāriṇa tāra adhare danta cāpi
<P>gadā bulāi bitrame cālai mahakopī | 77 |
<P>puṇa puṇa gadā bulāi prahāra karai bhūmi
<P>tu mahāpaṇḍita ẏehā bicāra kara svāmī | 78 |
<P>śuṇi dhr̥tarāṣṭa biduraku boilā
<P>aṇakopī ta bhāroimalla arjuna kemanta hoi galā | 79 |
<P>bidura boile deba śuṇa jagatādhi
<P>arjunara śarīra deba aṭai baḍa trodhī | 80 |
<P>bāmabhmaje dhanu troṇa dakṣine bālimuṭhi
<P>bhūmiki ātroṣiṇa cālai kopa dr̥ṣṭi | 81 |
<P>indra praśaste bāli biñchigalā pārthe
<P>dvādaśa yojana suranadī pariyante | 82 |
<P>ambikāra nandana puna bacana prakāśi
<P>nakuḷara bāratā bābu kehneka kahasi | 83 |
<P>nakuḷara kopa svāmī ki karibā anta
<P>ūrddhvabāhu kari kare bulābai konta | 84 |
<P1>81|2 bāma bhmajaku chāhiṁ bhūmiki kare dr̥ṣṭi | (keteka pothi)
[MBO-04(1)-8]
<P>bhmamiki māri chatra ākāra kari toḷi
<P>ātroṣi locane se bhūmiki chāhāṁi niroḷi | 85 |
<P>śuṇi dhr̥tarāṣṭa pacārai bacana
<P>kahasi bidura sahadebara gamana | 86 |
<P>binaẏa bhābe bidura dhr̥tarāṣṭe boilā
<P>hastināku cāhiṁ mantrībara caudiga ātrokṣilā | 87 |
<P>svāmī suranadīre nābe basibāra beḷe
<P>dropatīṁki binoi ye boile sakaḷe | 88 |
<P>banabāsa kāḷe kimpe keśa tora mukuḷā
<P>ẏehā bandhana kara go dr̥padara dulāḷā | 89 |
<P>byāsa ādikari se na kalā kāhā bola
<P>dropatīṁki binoi ye boile sakaḷe | 88 |
<P>banabāsa kāḷe kimpe keśa tora mukuḷā
<P>ẏehā bandhana kara go dr̥padara dulāḷā | 89 |
<P>byāsa ādikari se na kalā kāhā bola
<P>tu mahābhigyaṁ ẏehā bicāra manda bhai | 90 |
<P>dhr̥tarāṣṭa boile bābu śuṇa re bidura
<P>sampada birthe ābara kisa sodara | 91 |
<P>bābu tu ye boilu pāṇḍabaṁkara nāhiṁ birasa
<P>pratagyāṁ chāḍile ki sehi pauroṣa | 92 |
<P>muhiṁ bicārili pāṇḍabaṁkara kopa nāhiṁ
<P>tohora bacane mohora śarīra kampai | 93 |
<P>puṇa puṇa bicārai dhr̥tarāṣṭa mahārāẏe
<P>ẏekānta kari sannidhye hakārile saṁjaẏe | 94 |
<P>bābu bidura yāha kahilā muṁ hejilaiṁ hr̥de
<P>tu tāhā kemanta prāẏa maṇilu sohodre | 95 |
<P>gālabara nandana dhr̥tarāṣṭaku prakāśa
<P>samada haraṇe ābara kisa haraṣa | 96 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi galā ye mathāẏe odā basra dei
<P>gāndhārī puanta kāḷe ẏehimati triẏā ghenimaiṁ mihiṁ | 97 |
<P>bhīma abaśya kaurobaku māriba niśaṁku
<P>ẏehānte kāraṇa karibāku dhātā srijitā nāhiṁki muku | 98 |
[MBO-04(1)-9]
<P>svāmī yujheṣṭha ẏeteka śuṇikari hr̥de
<P>odābasra śire dei banabāsa galā hāde | 99 |
<P>śuṇa he dhr̥tarāṣṭa bhīmasenara kathā
<P>bairiki tāpapaṇa tāra chāḍai ki sarbathā | 100 |
<P>gadā bulāi yāuacchi ye bhūmiki ātreṣi
<P>gāndhārī puaku māribi banastaru āsi | 101 |
<P>arjuna bhūmire ye puṇi buṇigala bāli
<P>ẏehimiti sāṁgrāmare śara br̥ṣṭi karibi boli | 102 |
<P>bāli prāẏa kari karibi śara br̥ṣṭi
<P>abaśya samara hoiba kurukṣetra sr̥ṣṭi | 103 |
<P>sañjaẏa boilā deba śuṇimā dhr̥tarāṣṭra daṇḍadhārī
<P>nakuḷa bīra galā kunta ye ubhāri | 104 |
<P>ẏehimati kuntamune chatraprāẏa gunthi yokhi
<P>māribi kaurobanta ke pāriba rakhi | 105 |
<P>ẏehi konte ẏekā prahārake māribi daśabiṁśa
<P>bulāiṇa kontamuna āuṁsai niśa | 106 |
<P>sahadeba chāhiṁ yāhā se bulāiṇa aṅguṣṭhi
<P>caturddiga rājānta ẏethi marāiba dhr̥tirāṣṭi | 117 |
<P>sahadeba jāṇai gata āgata bhabiṣya
<P>banabāsuṁ aile ẏemanta hoiba abaśya | 108 |
<P>saṁjaẏa boile ẏeuṁ br̥kṣa ropi abaśya phaḷa bhmaṁji
<P>ati uttramilā phaḷa thiba ki mahīmaṇḍala teji | 109 |
<P>yehu sahiba se abaśya labhiba nā kāryya

<P>anubrate prāṇīṁki ta nohoi bipada

<H>{@duryyodhanara apamāna@}
<P>śakuni boilā deba śuṇimā kurupati
<P>pāṇḍabe ye banabāsa gale pañchukṣatrī | 1 |
<P>keuṇa sampade achanti paṇḍa putre

<P1>234| “māru abā rakhu praśurāmahuṁ āna nahiṁ” pāṭha pare
<>‘ṅa’ pothire bhinma pāṭha :–
<P1>āja āsi ke rakhiba rakhu re tumbhanta
<P1>pitā āgyāṁ meṇṭile mātāre bhagata | 1 |
<P1>praśurāma rāgeṇa uṭhile śirajhuṇi
<P1>raghurāma śira kopena pakāile hāṇi | 2 |
<P1>reṇukā dakṣine raghurāmara śira thoi

<P1>sumara haḷī āre iṣṭadebatā tohora
<P1>mātā pāiṁ gañjilu pitāku mohora | 4 |
<P1>haḷīorāma boile bhrātha aḷapa doṣaku
<P1>bahuta śāsti kiṁpe deuacha āmbhaṁku | 5 |
<P1>badhira na śuṇe yehne kambura śabada
<P1>paraśu kuṭhāre haḷī śira kale ccheda | 6 |
<P1>mātā pāśe thoile cchedana śira goṭi
<P1>leuṭiṇa nīḷarāma pāśe puṇi bheṭi | 7 |
<P1>nīḷarāma mukha chāhiṁ bolanti kupite
<P1>sumara re nīḷarāma to iṣṭa daibate | 8 |
<P1>nīḷarāma boile bhāi śuṇa praśurāma
<P1>kimarthe karucha tumbhe ẏeḍeka adharma | 9 |
<P1>kiṣa iṣṭa mora sumarabi deba svāmī
<P1>bikale nīḷa padmacaraṇe pariṇāmi | 10 |

<P>mahāyagyuṁ jāta kale janaka sādhu sādhu | 65 |
<P1>63| pañchadibasa, pañchabiṁśa dibasa, pāñchabaraṣa prabhr̥ti pāṭhāntaramāna
<>dekhāyāe |
[MBO-04(1)-64]
<P>āho rājana baikulya hoi yahuṁ māgile daśarathe

<P>puṇa puṇa jānakī ye dile bāli tinimuṭhi

<P>bālipiṇḍa bhmañji ye hoile suārtha

<>pare keteka pothire bhinmapāṭha :–

<P>baibasuta manu pachāranti agastiṁki
<P>arjuna ye aneka sebā kalāka ubongśīki | 1 |
<P>sehu puṇa kāraṇa pāilā ṭiki svarge

<P1>127|2 “kebaṇa bhmabane thāi satva raja tama”
<>pare ka, na, ṭa, ḍha, kha, śa, ja, jha pothire bhinma pāṭha :–
<P1>yujheṣṭhi debe boile satyuṁ jāta brahmā basai ākāśe
<P1>tamuṁjāta rudra ẏe basai madhyasvarga bāse |
<P1>rajaguṇuṁ jāta biṣṇu se basai pātāḷe
<P>brahmakarma dharma ẏe trisandhyāra kāḷe |
[MBO-04(1)-340]
<P>yujheṣṭha debe boile ẏe janme tuhi abā hoilu āsi baka
<P>bibeka guṇabanta tu baḍāi dhārmika | 137 |
<P>kāḷa boliṇa hāde yeuṁṇa puruṣa bichāra
<P>akṣaẏa abyaẏa abikāra aṇākāra | 138 |

<P>nāsikā cakṣu madhyare kara ho sandhāna | 139 |

<P>dvādaśamunā nārāja droṇaṁkara dilā
<P>yeuṁṇa nārāje tretaẏā yuge indra nāśagalā | 305 |
<P>se śara arjuna binddhalā ātreṣiṇa kari
<P>agni bāhāra hoilā baḷībelāḷa hr̥de paḍikari | 306 |
<P>se nārāja yahuṁ hr̥de paḍi hoilāka masiguṇḍā
<P>praśaṁsai dhanurjaẏe sādhu re puruṣaṣaṇā(?)  | 307 |
<P>keheneka kṣaṇe jātakalā tote keuṇa mahātmāṇī
<P>ye tote bīryyadilā sādhu sehi prāṇī | 308 |

<P>baḷībelāḷa upare paḍi sabonge hoileka cūri | 310 |

<P>baḷibelāḷa boilā bindha tora yeteka śahasra achai | 311 |

<P1>351|2 “mama doṣa aprādha kṣamā karibā debasvāmī”
<>pare “ṅa” pothire adhikā pāṭha :–
<P1>mātātahuṁ putra nirādhāra bākya śuṇi
<P1>bhīmasena caraṇe paḍilā puṇa puṇi |
<P1>saceta hoiṇa pachārai bhīmasena
<P1>pāde praṇapatya huẏe ẏe kāhāra nandana |
<P1>nāgeṇī boilā tumbhe śuṇa prāṇapati
<P1>putra doṣa kale pitā sahibā yugati |
[MBO-04(1)-386]
<P>na jāṇiṇa pitā kali kete doṣa muhiṁ

<P>āreka mandāẏeka pātile kapāḷī
<P>ṭaḷa ṭaḷa hoiṇa ye ṭaḷai basundharī | 111 |
<P>pr̥thibī boilā svāmī sambhāḷa biśvanātha
<P>ẏe mahārete hoibi nā rasāṅgata | 112 |
<P>māḍilāni mahābīryya dvādaśa juṇa pariyante
<P>basudhā baikulya dekhi kare dhaile biśvanāthe | 113 |
<P>mandākara arddheka deba kare chanti dhari
<P>kāhākaiṁ debā boli biśvanāthe bichāri | 114 |
<P>bhāḷiṇa boile deba pabana aputrika
<P>ẏeṇekaiṁ kāraṇa se pāiba aneka | 115 |
<P>paracaṇḍa pabanakaiṁ hakāriṇa bolanti paramayogī
<P>se mahābīryya tāhāra kare dile begi | 116 |
<P>ẏeṇe mokṣagati tuho pāibu maruta
<P>pabana boilā deba muṁho hoili kr̥tārtha | 117 |
<P>kare gheni bhāḷai ẏehā muṁ kisa karibi

[MBO-04(1)-405]
<P>pabana debatā gautamaṁka baṇī śuṇi
<P>aṣṭa dibaseke padārtheka maruta diai āṇi | 123 |
<P>teṇu kari triputi hoai tāhāra mana
<P>sanidhye prabeśa yāi hoile pabana | 124 |
<P>śuṇa go dropatī ahalyā kahile

<P>rudrara mahābīryya garbhare tāra paḍi

<P1>124|2 aṣṭadina ante prabeśa hoile pabana |–ḍa, ḍha

<P>bho pitā mātāra bhage na lāgu upastha
<P>yonire kemante muhiṁ hoibaiṁ jāta | 134 |
<P>pabana debatā yāiṁ kahile īśvaraṁku
<P>īśvare bajrakācheṭi dileka tāhāṁku | 135 |
<P>añjanīku bola ẏehā garbhagata karu

<P>parama yogī nāthara cihna pāiṇa kumara

<P1>134|2 “yonire kemante muhiṁ hoibaiṁ jāta”
<>pare ca, cha, ṇa, ja, ṭha pothire adhikā pāṭha :–
<P1>bho pitā mātāra bhage yebe nāgiba mora marma
<P1>yonire kemante muṁ hoibaiṁ janma |
<P1>ẏemanta bichāri kumara nohilāka janma
<P1>īśvaraṁka āge yāi kahilā pabana |
<P1>pabana kahante se jāṇile yogeśvara
<P1>mahā prama (parama) yogī se ye nohoi bāhāra |
<P1>īśvara mekhaḷi ye achai aṅgara
<P1>tahuṁ khaṇḍiẏeka ye dile debahara |
<P1>ẏehā nei dia ho añjanī hāthara
<P1>garbhaku kṣepuṁ putra hoiba abatāra |
<P1>pabana dlānei prabhañjanīra (añjanīra) hātha
<P1>takṣaṇe debī tāhā kale garbhagata |
<P1>garbhe thāiṇa tāhā jāṇilā kumara
<P1>kācheṭi kari tāhā pinddhalā kaṭira |
<P1>ahilā kahai ye dropatīṁka āgara
<P1>bajra kāchati pinddha hanumanta abatāra |
[MBO-04(1)-407]
<P>tuḷamāsa kr̥ṣṇapakṣa amābaira tithi
<P>arkabāra sedina nakṣatra ye svātī | 139 |
<P>bāḷaba nāme karaṇa śubha nāme yoga
<P>somaghare br̥haspati caturpāde bhoga | 140 |

<P>añjanī boilā re tu mohora bacha

<>‘ṭa’ pothira adhikā pāṭha–
<P1>debatāmāne āśa kariachanti yāhāra bāhāku
<P1>tuho daśaratha luchāilu ye tāhāku |

<P1>tāhāṁku luchāibāku nohoi tora dharma |

<P1>bhratha śatr̥ghana dilā muniṁka āgare |
<P1>daśaratha rājā caḷile anteśvara pure
<P1>bhratha śatr̥ ghanaku āṇidile ruṣiṁka chāmure |
<P1>tumbhe se aṭa ki rāma lakṣmaṇa beni bhrāta
<P1>muni boile re putra kahiba tumbhe sata |
<P1>muniṁkara agrate kahanti benibhāi
<P1>āmbhara nāma muni he bhratha śatr̥ ghana aṭai |
<P1>āmbhara jyeṣṭhabhrāta aṭanti śrīrāma
<P1>tāhāṁkara sānuja aṭanti lakṣaṇa |

<P1>begeṇa āna śrīrāma lakṣuṇa benibhrātha |
<P1>muniṁkara niṣṭhure daśaratha nr̥pamaṇi
<P1>śrīrāma lakṣmaṇaku sannidhye dile āṇi |
<P1>dekheṇa haraṣa hoile biśvāmitra
<P1>ẏehi se nirākāra biṣṇu aṭai daśaratha |

<P1>daśaratha boile mora jībanadhana ẏehi |
<P1>piṇḍa mo rahilā sāhā nelu biśvāmitra
<P1>ājahuṁ beni ākhi andha hoilā gādhiputra | (abaśiṣṭāṁśa parapr̥ṣṭhāre)

<H>{@gokarṇṇa tīrthara māhātmya@}
<P>ẏethu anantare caḷai dvijabara lajjā abhimāne
<P>prabeśa hoilā yāiṁ indrapraśasta bhmabane | 1 |
<P>dhuśāsana śakuni karṇṇa achanti ye basi
<P>gauramukha brāhmaṇa ẏemantara samaẏe prabeśilā āsi | 2 |
<P>dhuśāsana boilā paṇḍāẏe gala pāṇḍabanta ṭhābakari
<P>tumbhara galārata hoilāni māsa chāri | 3 |
<P>paṇḍāẏe keuṁṇa rājye dekhila pāṇḍabanta
<P>keuṁṇa bhābe dekhila achanti tāhānta | 4 |
<P>paṇḍāẏe boile āmbhe aneka durgama patha galu
<P>pañchāṇoi dibase yāiṁ pāṇḍabanta ṭhābakalu | 5 |
<P>āmbhe ẏethuṁ galuṁ jyeṣṭha kr̥ṣṇa pañchamī dinare
<P>tāhānta bheṭilu siṁgha śukaḷa sapatamī dinare | 6 |
<P>ẏemante pañchāṇoi dibasa āmbhara yāānte
<P>mote cihni nuārile pāṇḍaba pñchu bhrāthe | 7 |
<P>aṭhāaśi sahasra ruṣi achanti saṅgara
<P>purāṇa kahuchanti yujheṣṭhi āgara | 8 |
<P>gaṇḍā mr̥ga māriṇa ruṣiṁku dianti bhojī
<P>kandamūḷa āhāra sampoḍe citta bhaji | 9 |
<P>askanda bane ye rahiachanti pāṇḍaba
<P>āmbhanta dekhikari tāhāṁkara aneka daẏābhāba | 10 |
<P>aneka mate āmbhanta yācanti bhojana
<P>apāra kaṣaṇa kalu paṇḍura nandana | 11 |
<P>chadrama rūpa cihni nuārile paṇḍubāḷe
<P>apāra kaṭāḷa kari māgilu cūtaphaḷe | 12 |
